- **api:** `GET /v1/anchors?include=state` join + `/controls` real state cells ([#104](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/104)) — additive `?include=state` query parameter on `GET /v1/anchors` returns the anchor catalog LEFT JOINed to the tenant's worst-state-wins per-anchor rollup over the slice-012 `control_evaluations` ledger. Implemented as a **single CTE+join SQL query** — explicitly NOT a per-anchor loop calling `eval.Engine.ControlState` (the slice exists to avoid the 1,400-call fan-out anti-pattern that slice 098 surfaced). The CTE picks the latest evaluation per (tenant, control, scope_cell) via `DISTINCT ON` (mirrors slice 012's `ListLatestControlEvaluations` pattern), then aggregates worst-state-wins per anchor: `fail` > `inconclusive` > `pass` > `na` for the result column, `expired` > `stale` > `no_evidence` > `fresh` for freshness, `MAX` for `last_observed_at`. Anchors with no tenant control return `state: null` (the empty-state branch is honest — no fabrication, slice 098 P0-A1 carries through). Wire shape: `{anchors: [{...anchorWire, state: stateWire | null}]}` — additive; callers that omit `?include=state` continue to receive the v1 anchor-only shape unchanged. Both the latest-version list path and the `?framework_version_id=` path support the extension. Backend constitutional invariants honored: #6 (RLS — the join runs in a `tenancy.ApplyTenant` transaction, integration test asserts Tenant A's request never sees Tenant B's state); #2 (engine is sole writer of `control_evaluations` — this is a pure read over the engine's output table, not a parallel computation); #1 (rollup is per ANCHOR, not per framework). Frontend: `web/lib/api.ts` adds `AnchorWithState` + `listAnchorsWithState`; `web/app/api/controls/route.ts` (BFF) now calls the joined endpoint; `web/app/(authed)/controls/page.tsx` removes the `state: null` placeholder mapping and renders real state cells (the `—` placeholder remains for the legitimate null-state branch). New Go unit tests at `internal/api/anchors/state_unit_test.go` (5 cases: pass-through, no-control-null, no-observation, two-controls-pre-aggregated, include-parser); new Go integration tests at `internal/api/anchors/state_integration_test.go` (4 cases: omitted-include shape, empty-tenant null branch, worst-state-wins + RLS round-trip Tenant A vs Tenant B, design-doc column set); new vitest case in `web/app/api/controls/route.test.ts` pinning the joined-shape pass-through. JUDGMENT-type slice — decisions log at `docs/audit-log/104-anchors-include-state-decisions.md` records the 9 design calls. Spillover from slice 098.
- **frontend:** `/controls` list view + shared list shell ([#098](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/098)) — closes audit finding F-4 (the `/controls` link in the sidebar previously 404'd). New page at `web/app/(authed)/controls/page.tsx` renders the SCF anchor library as a table per the design captured in slice 093 (`Plans/mockups/controls.html` + `Plans/canvas/12-ui-fill-in-design-decisions.md` §1/2/3/7/8). Row source is `anchorWire` from `GET /v1/anchors` via a new tenant-scoped BFF at `web/app/api/controls/route.ts` (slice 094 cookie→bearer pattern). The page consumes the **new reusable list shell** at `web/components/list/` — five generic primitives (`ListPage`, `FilterPills`, `ListTable`, `EmptyState`, `ListLoadingSkeleton`) intentionally scoped domain-agnostic so the next four list-view slices (099 evidence / 100 risks / 101 policies / 102 audits) consume them from a single barrel import. Filter row is horizontal pills (P0-A2: no left sidebar); loading is 3 shimmer rows (P0-A3: no spinner); empty-state copy "No controls match these filters" with `Clear filters` CTA (filter-induced — every tenant has SCF anchors). State columns (`result` / `freshness_status` / `last_observed_at`) render `—` honestly until backend extension lands — slice 098 D1 records the gap, **spillover slice 104** files `GET /v1/anchors?include=state` to lift the per-row fan-out anti-pattern that the slice text itself rejected (1,400 anchors × per-row state call). Vitest covers the row-narrowing + filter-state computation (16 tests at `web/app/(authed)/controls/filters.test.ts`) and the BFF route (3 tests at `web/app/api/controls/route.test.ts`). Playwright spec at `web/e2e/controls-list.spec.ts` follows the slice-079 quarantine pattern pending the slice-082 seed-data harness. AFK-type slice.
- **frontend:** Compliance calendar with ICS export ([#094](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/094)) — cross-business view of upcoming compliance dates at `/calendar`. Aggregates four event types only (audit periods, exception expirations, policy reviews, periodic control reviews) per P0-A1; per-evidence-record freshness drift and framework-version supersession are deliberately out of scope. Backend: new `internal/api/calendar/` with three handlers (`GET /v1/calendar` JSON list, `GET /v1/calendar.ics` RFC 5545 feed, `POST /v1/calendar/subscription` token mint). ONE UNION ALL query in `internal/db/queries/calendar.sql` over `audit_periods` + `exceptions` + `policies` + `controls` (with a LEFT JOIN LATERAL onto `control_evaluations` for `last_evaluated_at`). Cadence math derives `next_due_at = last_evaluated_at + cadence_interval` where the cadence interval is the same `FreshnessMaxAge` mapping the slice-012 evaluation engine uses (one source of truth — decision D1). Default to rolling-window (D2). Never-evaluated control with a defined cadence emits an event at `now()` with `status=overdue` per AC-2c. ICS auth is a per-user opaque URL token (D3): `POST /v1/calendar/subscription` mints a random 32-byte token via `credstore.Issue`, stores `sha256(token)` in `api_keys`, scopes via `AllowedKinds=[calendar.read.v1]` so a leaked calendar URL token cannot be used as a general bearer; the calendar.ics handler is exempt from the upstream bearer-header middleware and authenticates the URL token inline. New migration `20260516000002_policies_next_review_at.sql` adds `policies.next_review_at TIMESTAMPTZ NULL` (D4) — no change to existing write paths; operators populate the value directly or via a future admin UI. RLS enforced at the DB layer (slice 033 pattern); integration test ISC-94-1/94-2 asserts cross-tenant isolation on both the exception and control-cadence paths. Truncation flag fires at the 500-event ceiling with a `next_from` cursor (D7). Frontend: new `/calendar` route under `web/app/(authed)/calendar/page.tsx` with hand-rolled agenda + month-grid views (no calendar-library dependency per P0-A6 / D6), URL-driven type filter, overdue-cue red dot for control events, "Subscribe in calendar" button copies the ICS URL to clipboard. New top-nav entry between Dashboard and Metrics (D8). BFF proxies under `web/app/api/calendar/{route.ts, subscription/route.ts}` follow the slice-040 pattern. Vitest covers both BFF routes (5 tests). Go integration tests (7 tests) cover RLS isolation, cadence math both branches, truncation, ICS validity, and ICS auth rejection cases. Playwright spec at `web/e2e/calendar.spec.ts` follows the slice-079 quarantine pattern pending the slice-082 seed-data harness. AFK-type slice — decisions log at `docs/audit-log/094-compliance-calendar-decisions.md` records the 8 design calls.
- **frontend:** Metrics dashboard + cascade-tree view ([#097](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/097)) — the frontend that consumes the slice-076 metrics-catalog backbone. New route `/dashboards/metrics` shows board-level metric cards (latest value, target, 90-day SVG sparkline, color-coded threshold badge); each card expands a vertical indent-and-rule cascade tree (decision D1) walking `GET /v1/metrics/cascade?level=board&depth=3` and reassembling the flat node list into a tree client-side. New route `/dashboards/metrics/[id]` shows the metric definition, immediate parents/children, the observation series as an inline-SVG line chart with target/warning/critical horizontal overlays, the target configuration panel, and a manual-input audit-trail. Admin-only `Submit value` modal (decision D3) gated via `getSessionMe().is_admin` (reuses the slice-043 pattern) that POSTs to `/v1/metrics/{id}/inputs` and invalidates the per-metric observation query so the new row appears immediately. Backend additive only — no slice-076 API changes (P0-A1). No new chart-library dependency (decision D2): inline-SVG sparkline + line-chart components colocated under `web/components/dashboards-metrics/` using shadcn theme tokens. New BFF routes under `web/app/api/metrics/**` follow the slice-040 dashboardProxy pattern. New shadcn Dialog primitive at `web/components/ui/dialog.tsx` wrapping `@base-ui/react/dialog`. Vitest suite at `web/lib/api/metrics.test.ts` covers the pure cascade-tree reassembly + threshold-badge color logic (22 tests, all green). Playwright spec at `web/e2e/metrics-dashboard.spec.ts` follows the slice-079 quarantine pattern pending the slice-082 seed-data harness. JUDGMENT-type slice — decisions log at `docs/audit-log/097-metrics-dashboard-cascade-view-decisions.md` records the three subjective calls.
- **catalog:** Metrics catalog + cascade + observation store ([#076](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/076)) — 5-table data model (`metrics_catalog`, `metric_cascade_edges`, `metric_observations`, `metric_targets`, `metric_inputs`) seeded from 8 YAML files at `catalogs/metrics/` (40 curated metrics across board / program / team cascades). 8 starter Go evaluators in `internal/metrics/eval/` run on a 15-minute cron (`ATLAS_METRICS_INTERVAL` env override). Read/write API: `GET /v1/metrics`, `GET /v1/metrics/cascade`, `GET /v1/metrics/{id}`, `GET /v1/metrics/{id}/observations`, `POST /v1/metrics/{id}/inputs`, `GET /v1/metrics/{id}/target`, `PUT /v1/metrics/{id}/target`. Insert trigger on `metric_inputs` replicates each manual entry to `metric_observations` so reads serve a unified series. Singleton-tenant-agnostic RLS pattern (slice 068) for the catalog + edges; four-policy RLS for tenant-scoped tables; append-only RLS for observations + inputs. Mkdocs site gains a "Measuring your program" page + an auto-generated reference (`just metrics-reference`). Follow-on dashboard slice filed at #097 (slice doc's 078 reference was stale). JUDGMENT-type slice — decisions log at `docs/audit-log/076-metrics-catalog-cascade-decisions.md` records the 16 design calls.
- **infra:** Security HTTP headers middleware ([#087](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/087)) — new `internal/api/securityheaders/` package applied as the FIRST `root.Use(...)` in the chi chain. Sets HSTS, X-Content-Type-Options, X-Frame-Options, Referrer-Policy on every response (including 401s + auth-exempt `/health` + `/auth/*` + `/login`). CSP ships as `Content-Security-Policy-Report-Only` initially (Next.js inline-script hydration would violate `script-src 'self'` enforcement); the trajectory toward enforced mode is documented in `docs/audit-log/087-security-http-headers-middleware-decisions.md`. Remediates the MEDIUM-HIGH finding from the 2026-Q2 security audit.
- **infra:** Dependency vulnerability scanning ([#089](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/089)) — three new informational CI jobs in `.github/workflows/ci.yml`: `Go · govulncheck` (Go call-graph-aware CVE detection, pinned `govulncheck@v1.1.3`), `Frontend · npm audit` (runtime-shipped JS deps in `web/`, `--omit=dev --audit-level=high`), and `Container · Trivy scan` (OS-package CVEs in the locally-built atlas image, `aquasecurity/trivy-action@0.28.0` with `ignore-unfixed: true`). All three follow the slice-061/069 stub-job pattern and are NOT added to `.github/branch-protection.json`'s required-checks list — promotion-to-required is a future slice once cadence + false-positive rate are observed. HIGH+CRITICAL is the unified fail threshold. Reports upload as workflow artifacts for maintainer triage. Per-scanner suppression mechanism + threshold rationale documented in `docs/audit-log/089-dependency-vulnerability-scanning-decisions.md`. Remediates the MEDIUM finding from the 2026-Q2 security audit (the last open finding from that audit).
- **frontend:** Mockups for six missing top-level pages ([#093](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/093)) — six static HTML wireframes added under `Plans/mockups/` for the previously-404'ing top-level routes: `controls.html`, `evidence.html`, `risks.html`, `policies.html`, `audits.html`, `settings.html`. Each mockup is a self-contained Tailwind-via-CDN file matching the existing dashboard/board-pack chrome (sticky top-bar + 56px left sidebar + main panel with horizontal filter row + table + empty state + loading skeleton). All column sets derived from verified backend wire shapes (`anchorWire` + `stateWire`, `recordWire` + `receiptWire`, `riskWire`, `policyWire` + `rateResponse`, `periodWire`, `me/*` + `admincreds.ListItem`) per P0-A5; no invented endpoints. The dashboard sidebar is updated to the new canonical nav order (Dashboard · Controls · Evidence · Risks · Audits · Policies · Vendors · Board Packs · Settings · Admin) so the user sees consistent placement when navigating by mockup-flipping; the four sidebar-less mockups (control / board-pack / questionnaire) are unchanged per P0-A3. `Plans/mockups/index.html` gains a "v1 fill-in pages" section with one tile per mockup, each marked "design only — implementation pending". Design decisions captured in `Plans/canvas/12-ui-fill-in-design-decisions.md` (top-nav order rationale, empty-state + loading-skeleton patterns, /settings user-only vs /admin tenant scope, /risks list vs /risks/hierarchy co-existence, /audits plural vs /audit/[controlId] singular). Unblocks six follow-up per-page implementation slices to be drafted post-merge.

### Changed

- **infra:** sqlc toolchain pinned to v1.31.1 + regen reset ([#109](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/109)) — closes the slice 106 P1 finding ("sqlc toolchain drift produces silent regen regressions"). `SQLC_VERSION := "v1.31.1"` pinned in `justfile`; new `sqlc-version-check` recipe gated as a dependency of `sqlc-generate`; CLAUDE.md tech-stack table + CONTRIBUTING.md Prerequisites + Local CI parity subsection all reference the pin. Root cause documented in `docs/audit-log/109-sqlc-toolchain-pin-decisions.md`: slice 065 wrapped `CREATE TYPE` in idempotent `DO $$ BEGIN ... END $$;` blocks for self-host bundle re-apply safety, but sqlc v1.31.1 cannot parse `CREATE TYPE` inside a DO block — every enum-typed SELECT column degrades to `interface{}` on regen, dropping typed enum constants downstream callers depend on. Fix: new tool-input-only file `internal/db/sqlc-schema/_enums.sql` declares every enum as a bare `CREATE TYPE` and is listed FIRST in `sqlc.yaml`'s `schema:` array (NEVER applied to a live DB; the justfile migration runner globs `migrations/sql/*.sql` only). The DO-block re-declarations that follow are silently tolerated as duplicates by sqlc. Slice 076's `internal/db/dbx/models_metrics.go` hand-split is RETIRED — the regen places metric types back into the canonical `models.go`. Two narrow hand-narrows preserved (`AckDenominator`/`AckNumerator` in `policies.sql.go` × slice 107; `StateResult`/`StateFreshnessStatus` × 2 row types in `scf_anchors.sql.go` × slice 104) — each annotated in place with a pointer to the decisions log. Slice 106's hand-extension of `ListEvidencePaged` is retired; the natural sqlc-emitted form is now canonical. New informational CI job `Go · sqlc generate diff` added with `continue-on-error: true` (NOT in required-checks per P0-A3). No behavioral change — `go test ./...` passes with zero test edits.

- **infra:** Pre-push hook now also runs `npm run lint -w web` ([#083](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/083)) — follow-on to slice 081 D3. Adds a `local` `npm-lint-web` hook to `.pre-commit-config.yaml` (`stages: [pre-push]`, `files: ^web/`, `language: system`, `pass_filenames: false`) so frontend ESLint errors block locally before CI's `Frontend · lint` job (slice 078) catches them. Hook is skipped on backend-only pushes via the `^web/` files predicate. Emergency bypass via `git push --no-verify` is unchanged (P0-A1). Decisions log at `docs/audit-log/083-pre-push-hook-add-lint-decisions.md` records the AC-3 deliberate-failure test result (`react/jsx-key` error → push exit code 1, push not transmitted).
- **frontend:** Root route `/` now redirects instead of rendering the stock create-next-app template that shipped with the slice-005 scaffold ([#091](https://github.com/mgoodric/security-atlas/issues/091)). Server-component handler at `web/app/page.tsx` reads `SESSION_COOKIE` from `@/lib/auth` and emits a 307 to `/dashboard` for authenticated requests, `/login?from=/` for unauthenticated requests. Two destinations only — no third "/onboarding" branch (P0-A2). No client-side JS, no rendered UI, no Vercel/Next.js branding remains. New Playwright spec at `web/e2e/root-redirect.spec.ts` asserts both branches at the 307-response level plus a belt-and-suspenders navigation-follow case; uses neutral `test-*` fixture tokens only (P0-A7). Stock-template SVGs were already absent from `web/public/` at slice start (AC-6 no-op). Verified locally: `curl -I http://localhost:3015/` returns 307 → `/login?from=%2F`; with `Cookie: sa_session_token=…` returns 307 → `/dashboard`.
### Fixed

- **infra (slice 088):** atlas-cli outbound HTTP calls now carry an explicit per-call timeout via the new `cmd/atlas-cli/cmdhttp` package (10s for feature-flag reads, 30s for credential reset-bootstrap). Resolves the Q2 2026 security audit MEDIUM finding — the package-level-default HTTP client has no timeout and a hung atlas server would previously stall the CLI indefinitely. AC-4 grep gate enforces zero residual package-level-default-client references under `cmd/atlas-cli/`.
- **infra (slice 092):** version display end-to-end fix. Two bugs combined to make the deployed UI's footer report `v(none)` / `unknown`: (a) `.github/workflows/container-publish.yml`'s `docker/build-push-action@v7` step did not pass `build-args` for `VERSION`/`COMMIT`/`BUILD_TIME`, so the Dockerfile's `dev`/`none`/`unknown` defaults were baked into every published image; (b) `web/proxy.ts` (the Next.js 16 request interceptor, renamed from `middleware.ts`) had no exemption for `/api/version`, so every BFF call to the intentionally-public version endpoint returned 307 → `/login`. The workflow now passes all three build-args from `steps.meta.outputs.version` + `github.sha` + a computed RFC3339 UTC `BUILD_TIME`; `proxy.ts` exempts exactly `/api/version` (exact-equality match, P0-A1 forbids broadening). New vitest unit test at `web/proxy.test.ts` (10 cases enumerating the exempt path + adjacent-prefix attack surface + the AC-7 negative case `/api/admin/me` still 307s) plus new Playwright e2e at `web/e2e/version-public.spec.ts`. AC-3 reduces to "verify on first release after merge" — the publish-time smoke deferred to keep the diff minimal per the slice scope. Decisions log: `docs/audit-log/092-version-display-end-to-end-decisions.md`.
